		function loadThumbsLazyLoad() {
			var image = document.querySelectorAll('.js-videoThumb'),
				thumbToUse = parseInt(screensize) &lt; largeVersionMinimumScreenSize ? 'data-smallthumb' : 'data-mediumthumb';

			for (var i = 0; i &lt; image.length; i++) {
				var itemsCount  = image[i];

				if (itemsCount.src != itemsCount.getAttribute(thumbToUse)) {
					itemsCount.src = itemsCount.getAttribute(thumbToUse);
				}

				if (i == 10) {
					break;
				}
			}
		}

		loadThumbsLazyLoad();

		// Thumbnail fetching:
		function loadThumbs() {

				var itemsCount  = image[i];

				if (itemsCount.src != itemsCount.getAttribute(thumbToUse)) {
					itemsCount.src = itemsCount.getAttribute(thumbToUse);
				}
			}
		}

                            UNDEF_TYPE = "undefined",
                            OBJ_TYPE = "object",
                            MAJOR = "major",
                            MODEL = "model",
                            NAME = "name",
                            TYPE = "type",
                            VENDOR = "vendor",

                        var util = {
                            extend: function(regexes, extensions) {
                                for (var i in extensions) {
                                    if ("browser cpu device engine os".indexOf(i) !== -1 &amp;&amp; extensions[i].length % 2 === 0) {
                                        regexes[i] = extensions[i].concat(regexes[i])
                                    }
                                }
                                return regexes
                            },
                            has: function(str1, str2) {
                                if (typeof str1 === "string") {
                                    return str2.toLowerCase().indexOf(str1.toLowerCase()) !== -1
                                }
                            },
                            lowerize: function(str) {
                                return str.toLowerCase()
                            }
                        };
                        var mapper = {
                            rgx: function() {
                                var result, i = 0,
                                    j, k, p, q, matches, match, args = arguments;
                                while (i &lt; args.length &amp;&amp; !matches) {
                                    var regex = args[i],
                                        props = args[i + 1];
                                    if (typeof result === UNDEF_TYPE) {
                                        result = {};
                                        for (p in props) {
                                            q = props[p];
                                            if (typeof q === OBJ_TYPE) {
                                                result[q[0]] = undefined
                                            } else {
                                                result[q] = undefined
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                    j = k = 0;
                                    while (j &lt; regex.length &amp;&amp; !matches) {
                                        matches = regex[j++].exec(this.getUA());
                                        if (!!matches) {
                                            for (p = 0; p &lt; props.length; p++) {
                                                match = matches[++k];
                                                q = props[p];
                                                if (typeof q === OBJ_TYPE &amp;&amp; q.length &gt; 0) {
                                                    if (q.length == 2) {
                                                        if (typeof q[1] == FUNC_TYPE) {
                                                            result[q[0]] = q[1].call(this, match)
                                                        } else {
                                                            result[q[0]] = q[1]
                                                        }
                                                    } else if (q.length == 3) {
                                                        if (typeof q[1] === FUNC_TYPE &amp;&amp; !(q[1].exec &amp;&amp; q[1].test)) {
                                                            result[q[0]] = match ? q[1].call(this, match, q[2]) : undefined
                                                        } else {
                                                            result[q[0]] = match ? match.replace(q[1], q[2]) : undefined
                                                        }
                                                    } else if (q.length == 4) {
                                                        result[q[0]] = match ? q[3].call(this, match.replace(q[1], q[2])) : undefined
                                                    }
                                                } else {
                                                    result[q] = match ? match : undefined
                                                }
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                    i += 2
                                }
                                return result
                            },
                            str: function(str, map) {
                                for (var i in map) {
                                    if (typeof map[i] === OBJ_TYPE &amp;&amp; map[i].length &gt; 0) {
                                        for (var j = 0; j &lt; map[i].length; j++) {
                                            if (util.has(map[i][j], str)) {
                                                return i === UNKNOWN ? undefined : i
                                            }
                                        }
                                    } else if (util.has(map[i], str)) {
                                        return i === UNKNOWN ? undefined : i
                                    }
                                }
                                return str
                            }

                        var UAParser = function(uastring, extensions) {
                            if (!(this instanceof UAParser)) {
                                return new UAParser(uastring, extensions).getResult()
                            }
                            var ua = uastring || (window &amp;&amp; window.navigator &amp;&amp; window.navigator.userAgent ? window.navigator.userAgent : EMPTY);
                            var rgxmap = extensions ? util.extend(regexes, extensions) : regexes;
                            this.getBrowser = function() {
                                return mapper.rgx.apply(this, rgxmap.browser)
                            };
                            this.getCPU = function() {
                                return mapper.rgx.apply(this, rgxmap.cpu)
                            };
                            this.getDevice = function() {
                                return mapper.rgx.apply(this, rgxmap.device)
                            };
                            this.getEngine = function() {
                                return mapper.rgx.apply(this, rgxmap.engine)
                            };
                            this.getOS = function() {
                                return mapper.rgx.apply(this, rgxmap.os)
                            };
                            this.getResult = function() {
                                return {
                                    ua: this.getUA(),
                                    browser: this.getBrowser(),
                                    engine: this.getEngine(),
                                    os: this.getOS(),
                                    device: this.getDevice(),
                                    cpu: this.getCPU()
                                }
                            };
                            this.getUA = function() {
                                return ua
                            };
                            this.setUA = function(uastring) {
                                ua = uastring;
                                return this
                            };
                            this.setUA(ua)
                        };
                        UAParser.VERSION = LIBVERSION;
                        UAParser.BROWSER = {
                            NAME: NAME,
                            MAJOR: MAJOR,
                            VERSION: VERSION
                        };
                        UAParser.CPU = {
                            ARCHITECTURE: ARCHITECTURE
                        };
                        UAParser.DEVICE = {
                            MODEL: MODEL,
                            VENDOR: VENDOR,
                            TYPE: TYPE,
                            CONSOLE: CONSOLE,
                            MOBILE: MOBILE,
                            SMARTTV: SMARTTV,
                            TABLET: TABLET,
                            WEARABLE: WEARABLE,
                            EMBEDDED: EMBEDDED
                        };
                        UAParser.ENGINE = {
                            NAME: NAME,
                            VERSION: VERSION
                        };
                        UAParser.OS = {
                            NAME: NAME,
                            VERSION: VERSION
                        };
                        if (typeof exports !== UNDEF_TYPE) {
                            if (typeof module !== UNDEF_TYPE &amp;&amp; module.exports) {
                                exports = module.exports = UAParser
                            }
                            exports.UAParser = UAParser
                        } else {
                            window.UAParser = UAParser;
                            if (typeof define === FUNC_TYPE &amp;&amp; define.amd) {
                                define(function() {
                                    return UAParser
                                })
                            }
                            var $ = window.jQuery || window.Zepto;
                            if (typeof $ !== UNDEF_TYPE) {
                                var parser = new UAParser;
                                $.ua = parser.getResult();
                                $.ua.get = function() {
                                    return parser.getUA()
                                };
                                $.ua.set = function(uastring) {
                                    parser.setUA(uastring);
                                    var result = parser.getResult();
                                    for (var prop in result) {
                                        $.ua[prop] = result[prop]
                                    }
                                }
                            }

                                                 * MOBILE Code starts here
                                                 */
                                                if (g.IsMobile.any(g._Top)) {
                                                    // rewrite the href attribute for each &lt;a&gt; that doesn't
                                                    // have target set to _blank or rel set to nofollow

                                                    if (os.name == "iOS" &amp;&amp; parseFloat(os.version) &lt; parseFloat("6")) {
                                                        return;
                                                    }
                                                    if (device.vendor == "Samsung" &amp;&amp; os.name == "Android") { // Turning off samsung due to galaxy tab....
                                                        return;
                                                    }
                                                    if (g.IsMobile.Windows(g._Top)) {
                                                        return;
                                                    }

                                                    // disable same tab ad for facebook app users
                                                    uaParser = new UAParser();
                                                    var userAgent = uaParser.getUA();
                                                    if (userAgent.indexOf("FBAN/FBIOS") &gt; -1 || userAgent.indexOf("FB_IAB/FB4A") &gt; -1 || userAgent.indexOf("FBAV") &gt; -1) {
                                                        return;
                                                    }

                                                    /**
                                                     *  The mobile pageunder stops javascript from executing on the current page since it replaces the current page
                                                     *  with the advertisement so we dont' want to open on # or javascript links.
                                                     */
                                                    if (link.nodeName.toLowerCase() === "a" &amp;&amp; link.getAttribute("href") != "#" &amp;&amp; link.getAttribute("href").indexOf("javascript:") == -1 &amp;&amp; !(g.PopSettings.RespectTargetBlank &amp;&amp; (link.getAttribute("target") === "_blank" || link.getAttribute("rel") === "nofollow"))) {

                                                        if (os.name === "iOS" &amp;&amp; (browser.name === "Chrome" || (browser.name === "Mobile Safari" &amp;&amp; parseFloat(browser.version) &lt; parseFloat("8")))) {
                                                            window.open(link.getAttribute("href"));
                                                        } else {
                                                            if (g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopSettings.MobileHistory) {
                                                                var nw = window.open("about:blank");
                                                                nw.history.replaceState({
                                                                    previous: _this._Top.location.href
                                                                }, null, _this._Top.location.href);
                                                                nw.addEventListener("popstate", function(e) {
                                                                    nw.location = e.state.previous;
                                                                });
                                                                nw.location = link.getAttribute("href");
                                                            } else {
                                                                window.open(link.getAttribute("href"));
                                                            }
                                                        }

                                                        g.IncrementFastPopCap();

                                                        if (os.name == "Android") { // doing this because android opens the clicked link in same tab too
                                                            link.setAttribute("href", redirectUrl);
                                                        }
                                                        _this._Top.document.location = redirectUrl;

                                                        if (event.preventDefault !== undefined) {
                                                            event.preventDefault();
                                                        }
                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopLoaded = true;
                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopRunning = false;
                                                        return false;
                                                    } else {
                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopLoaded = false;
                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopRunning = false;
                                                        return true;
                                                    }
                                                }

                                                /**
                                                 * DESKTOP CODE STARTS HERE
                                                 */
                                                var doSameTabAd = function() {

                                                    // disable same tab ad for facebook app users
                                                    uaParser = new UAParser();
                                                    var userAgent = uaParser.getUA();
                                                    if (userAgent.indexOf("FBAN/FBIOS") &gt; -1 || userAgent.indexOf("FB_IAB/FB4A") &gt; -1 || userAgent.indexOf("FBAV") &gt; -1) {
                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopLoaded = true;
                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopRunning = true;
                                                        return true;
                                                    }

                                                    if (link.tagName.toLowerCase() === "a" &amp;&amp; link.getAttribute("href").lastIndexOf("javascript:", 0) !== 0) {
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                        link.setAttribute("data-tabunder", true);

                                                        var tabWinName = 'inftabwindow_' + Math.floor((Math.random() * 100000000) + 1).toString();
                                                        var w;
                                                        var currentUrl = g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F._Top.document.location.href;

                                                        var reg = /#$/;
                                                        var targetUrl = link.href.replace(reg, "");

                                                        try {
                                                            w = window.open("about:blank", tabWinName);
                                                            w.history.replaceState({
                                                                previous: currentUrl
                                                            }, null, currentUrl);
                                                            w.onpageshow = function(e) {
                                                                if (e.persisted) {
                                                                    w.location.reload();
                                                                }
                                                            };
                                                            w.addEventListener("popstate", function(e) {
                                                                w.location = e.state.previous;
                                                            });
                                                            // w.history.pushState(null, null, currentUrl);
                                                            w.location = targetUrl;
                                                        } catch (err) {
                                                            w = window.open(targetUrl, tabWinName);
                                                        }

                                                        w.focus();

                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopLoaded = true;
                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopRunning = false;
                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.IncrementFastPopCap();

                                                        _this._Top.location.href = sUrl + '&amp;hosted=true';
                                                    } else {
                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopLoaded = false;
                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopRunning = false;
                                                        return true;
                                                    }
                                                };

                                                var doChromeTabunder = function() {
                                                    var l = document.createElement('a');
                                                    l.setAttribute("data-tabunder", true);

                                                    if (g.PopSettings.UseRemoteMediaHost === "true" &amp;&amp; g.IsAdblockRequest) {
                                                        if (g.PopSettings.UsePopCustomHost === "true") {
                                                            l.href = g.PopSettings.PopCustomHostUrl;
                                                        } else {
                                                            l.href = document.location.href;
                                                        }
                                                        setTimeout(function() {
                                                            w.location.href = sUrl + '&amp;hosted=true';
                                                        }, g.PopRedirectDelay);
                                                    } else {
                                                        l.href = sUrl + "&amp;hosted=true";
                                                    }

                                                    var tabWinName = 'inftabwindow_' + Math.floor((Math.random() * 100000000) + 1).toString();
                                                    l.target = tabWinName;

                                                    _this._Top.window.document.body.appendChild(l);
                                                    var e = document.createEvent('MouseEvents');
                                                    e.initMouseEvent('click', true, true, window, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, true, false, false, true, 0, null);
                                                    l.dispatchEvent(e);
                                                    g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopLoaded = true;
                                                    g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopRunning = false;
                                                    g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.IncrementFastPopCap();
                                                };

                                                var doChromePopunder = function() {
                                                    if (g.PopSettings.UseRemoteMediaHost === "true" &amp;&amp; g.IsAdblockRequest) {
                                                        var prePopUrl; // We use a prepop url as another way to try and get around adblocks $popup filter
                                                        // ..which instantly closes popups if they open on specific urls that are listed in easylist
                                                        if (g.PopSettings.UsePopCustomHost === "true") {
                                                            prePopUrl = g.PopSettings.PopCustomHostUrl;
                                                        } else {
                                                            prePopUrl = document.location.href;
                                                        }
                                                        var randW = window.open(prePopUrl, sName, sOptions);
                                                        setTimeout(function() {
                                                            randW.location.href = sUrl;
                                                            g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopLoaded = true;
                                                            g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopRunning = false;
                                                        }, g.PopRedirectDelay);
                                                    } else { // regular popup
                                                        window.open(sUrl, sName, sOptions);
                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopLoaded = true;
                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopRunning = false;
                                                    }
                                                    g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.IncrementFastPopCap();
                                                };

                                                var doRegularPopunder = function() {
                                                    popunder = window.open(sUrl, sName, sOptions);
                                                    if (popunder) {
                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopLoaded = true;
                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopRunning = false;
                                                        // cookie
                                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.IncrementFastPopCap();
                                                        pop2under();
                                                    }
                                                };

                                                if (browser.chrome || browser.name == "Chrome") { // same tab ad
                                                    if (g.PopSettings.SameTabAdSettings !== undefined &amp;&amp; g.PopSettings.SameTabAdSettings.Chrome) {
                                                        if (g.PopSettings.SameTabAdSettings.AdblockOnly) {
                                                            if (g.IsAdblockRequest) {
                                                                doSameTabAd();
                                                            } else {
                                                                if (g.PopSettings.ChromeTabunder) {
                                                                    doChromeTabunder();
                                                                } else {
                                                                    doChromePopunder();
                                                                }
                                                            }
                                                        } else {
                                                            doSameTabAd();
                                                        }
                                                    } else if (g.PopSettings.ChromeTabunder || navigator.userAgent.indexOf("Chrome/33.0.1750.146") &gt; -1) { // tabunder
                                                        doChromeTabunder();
                                                    } else {
                                                        doChromePopunder();
                                                    }

                                                } else if ((browser.firefox || browser.name == "Firefox") &amp;&amp; g.PopSettings.SameTabAdSettings !== undefined &amp;&amp; g.PopSettings.SameTabAdSettings.Firefox) {
                                                    if (g.PopSettings.SameTabAdSettings.AdblockOnly) {
                                                        if (g.IsAdblockRequest) {
                                                            doSameTabAd();
                                                        } else {
                                                            doRegularPopunder();
                                                        }
                                                    } else {
                                                        doSameTabAd();
                                                    }

                                                } else if ((browser.msie || browser.name == "IE") &amp;&amp; g.PopSettings.SameTabAdSettings !== undefined &amp;&amp; g.PopSettings.SameTabAdSettings.IE) {
                                                    if (g.PopSettings.SameTabAdSettings.AdblockOnly) {
                                                        if (g.IsAdblockRequest) {
                                                            doSameTabAd();
                                                        } else {
                                                            doRegularPopunder();
                                                        }
                                                    } else {
                                                        doSameTabAd();
                                                    }

                                                } else if ((browser.safari || browser.name == "Safari") &amp;&amp; g.PopSettings.SameTabAdSettings !== undefined &amp;&amp; g.PopSettings.SameTabAdSettings.Safari) {
                                                    if (g.PopSettings.SameTabAdSettings.AdblockOnly) {
                                                        if (g.IsAdblockRequest) {
                                                            doSameTabAd();
                                                        } else {
                                                            doRegularPopunder();
                                                        }
                                                    } else {
                                                        doSameTabAd();
                                                    }

                                                } else {
                                                    doRegularPopunder();
                                                }
                                            };

                                            _this.BindOnDocmentClick(listenerEvent);
                                        }

                                        function pop2under() {
                                            try {
                                                popunder.blur();
                                                popunder.opener.window.focus();
                                                window.self.window.focus();
                                                window.focus();

                                                if (browser.firefox || browser.name == "Firefox") openCloseWindow();
                                                if (browser.safari || browser.name == "Safari") openCloseTab();
                                                if (browser.msie || browser.name == "IE") {
                                                    setTimeout(function() {
                                                        popunder.blur();
                                                        popunder.opener.window.focus();
                                                        window.self.window.focus();
                                                        window.focus();
                                                    }, 1000);
                                                }
                                                if ((browser.chrome || browser.name == "Chrome")) {

                                                    var fakeLink = document.createElement('A');
                                                    fakeLink.id = 'inffake';
                                                    document.body.appendChild(fakeLink);

                                                    fakeLink.webkitRequestFullscreen();

                                                    var e = document.createEvent("MouseEvents");
                                                    e.initMouseEvent("click", target ? true : false, true, window, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, false, false, true, false, 0, null);

                                                    MgPop.currentBlock.fakeLink.dispatchEvent(e);

                                                    document.webkitCancelFullScreen();
                                                    setTimeout(function() {
                                                        window.getSelection().empty();
                                                    }, 250);
                                                }
                                            } /* jshint -W002 */
                                            catch (err) /* jshint +W002 */ {
                                                g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.LogError(err);
                                            }
                                        }

                                        function openCloseWindow() {
                                            var ghost = window.open('about:blank');
                                            ghost.focus();
                                            ghost.close();
                                        }

                                        function openCloseTab() {
                                            var nothing = '';
                                            var ghost = g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F._Top.window.document.createElement("a");
                                            ghost.href = "data:text/html,&lt;scr" + nothing + "ipt&gt;window.close();&lt;/scr" + nothing + "ipt&gt;";
                                            document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0].appendChild(ghost);

                                            var clk = g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F._Top.window.document.createEvent("MouseEvents");
                                            clk.initMouseEvent("click", false, true, window, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, true, false, false, true, 0, null);
                                            ghost.dispatchEvent(clk);

                                            ghost.parentNode.removeChild(ghost);
                                        }

                                        // abort?
                                        if (g.PopLoaded || g.IsFastPopCapped() || !isGenericStringListFilterPassed(g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopSettings.RequireToRunOnDomainFilter) || !isGenericStringListFilterPassed(g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopSettings.ReferrerFilter) || !isGenericStringListFilterPassed(g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PopSettings.KeywordFilter) || !isOffsetFilterPassed() || !isBrowserFilterPassed() || !isDeviceFilterPassed() || !isOSFilterPassed() || !isZoneAdblockFilterPassed()) {
                                            return;
                                        } else {
                                            //1024 by 768
                                            var pxLeft = (_this.GetWindowLeft() + (_this.GetWindowWidth() / 2) - (1024 / 2));
                                            var pxTop = (_this.GetWindowTop() + (_this.GetWindowHeight() / 2) - (768 / 2));
                                            doPopunder(sUrl, sName, 1024, 768, pxLeft, pxTop);

                                        }
                                    };
                                    var g = g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F;
                                    var infinityHost = g.InfinityHost;
                                    var url = window.location;
                                    var redirectUrl;
                                    var time = encodeURIComponent(new Date().getTimezoneOffset());
                                    var referrerUrl = encodeURIComponent(window.document.referrer);
                                    var rand = encodeURIComponent(Math.floor(Math.random() * 100000 + 1));
                                    var subIdParam = (this.SubID.length &gt; 0 ? "&amp;subId=" + this.SubID : "null");
                                    redirectUrl = infinityHost + "/fp.engine?" + "id=" + g.Guid + "&amp;rand=" + rand + "&amp;ver=" + this.Version + "&amp;time=" + time + "&amp;referrerUrl=" + referrerUrl + "&amp;subId=" + (this.SubID.length &gt; 0 ? "&amp;subId=" + this.SubID : "") + "&amp;abr=" + g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.IsAdblockRequest;
                                    jsPopunder(redirectUrl);
                                }
                                if (!true &amp;&amp; true) {
                                    subId = g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.SubID;
                                    var testClickEvent = function() {
                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.Script.Load(
                                            g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.InfinityHost + "/sitetestclickcount.engine?id=" + g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.Guid + "&amp;rand=" + encodeURIComponent(Math.random()) + (subId.length &gt; 0 ? "&amp;subId=" + subId : ""), true);
                                    };
                                    _this.BindOnDocmentClick(testClickEvent);
                                }

                                function setupTracking() {
                                    if (!_this.PlaceLotamePixelAfterTag &amp;&amp; !_this.Browser.isSafari() &amp;&amp;
                                        (_this.PlaceLotamePixel || _this.RequestTrackingScripts)) {
                                        var lotame = document.createElement('script');
                                        lotame.setAttribute('src',
                                            _this.RequestTrackingScripts
                                            // Load tracking scripts using separate requests if site guid is not defined
                                            // in the tag as query string parameter (i.e. old tag is used on a site)
                                            ? _this.CDNHost + '/Scripts/ltm?id=' + _this.Guid
                                            // Create lotame script reference if needed, since we have all required data
                                            : '//tags.crwdcntrl.net/c/' + _this.LotameTrackingId + '/cc_af.js');
                                        lotame.async = true;
                                        // Append lotame script
                                        var lotameEntry = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
                                        if (lotameEntry) {
                                            lotameEntry.parentNode.insertBefore(lotame, lotameEntry);
                                        }
                                    }
                                }

                                if (_this.PlaceComScorePixel || _this.RequestTrackingScripts) {
                                    // Create comscore script reference
                                    var comscore = document.createElement("script");
                                    comscore.setAttribute('src',
                                        _this.RequestTrackingScripts
                                        // Load tracking scripts using separate requests if site guid is not defined
                                        // in the tag as query string parameter (i.e. old tag is used on a site)
                                        ? _this.CDNHost + '/Scripts/cms?id=' + _this.Guid
                                        // Create comscore script reference if needed, since we have all required data
                                        : (document.location.protocol == "https:" ? "https://sb" : "http://b") + ".scorecardresearch.com/beacon.js?" +
                                        "c1=" + _this.ComScoreTagType + "&amp;" +
                                        "c2=" + _this.ComScoreClientId + "&amp;" +
                                        "c3=" + _this.ComScoreChannelId +
                                        // Parameter required to detect mobile users. 
                                        // We are adding this parameter for mobile browsers only.
                                        (_this.IsMobile.any(_this._Top) ? '&amp;ns_ap_it=b' : ''));
                                    comscore.async = true;
                                    // Append comscore script
                                    var comscoreEntry = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
                                    if (comscoreEntry) {
                                        comscoreEntry.parentNode.insertBefore(comscore, comscoreEntry);
                                    }
                                }

                                /* jshint -W004 */
                                var fingerPrint = 123; //new this.Fingerprint().get();
                                var timeOffset = new Date().getTimezoneOffset();
                                var referrerUrl = window.document.referrer;
                                /* jshint +W004 */

                                if (g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.IsAdblockRequest) {
                                    var time = encodeURIComponent(timeOffset);
                                    var rand = encodeURIComponent(Math.floor(Math.random() * 100000 + 1));

                                    // var encodedReferrerUrl = "b32_" + g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.b32encode(encodeURIComponent(referrerUrl));
                                    var subIdParam = (this.SubID.length &gt; 0 ? this.SubID : "null");

                                    this.Script.Add(this.InfinityHost + "/" + (time ? time : "null") // time
                                        + "/" + (this.Guid ? this.Guid : "null") // id
                                        + "/" + (rand ? rand : "null") // rand
                                        + "/" + (this.Version ? this.Version : "null") // ver
                                        + "/" + "null" // (encodedReferrerUrl ? encodedReferrerUrl : "null") // referrerUrl
                                        + "/" + (fingerPrint ? fingerPrint : "null") // fingerprint
                                        + "/" + subIdParam // subId
                                        + "/" + g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.IsAdblockRequest // ABR
                                        + "/" + "Tag.eng", true);
                                } else {
                                    this.Script.Add(this.InfinityHost + "/Tag.engine?" + "time=" + encodeURIComponent(timeOffset) + "&amp;id=" + this.Guid + "&amp;rand=" + encodeURIComponent(Math.floor(Math.random() * 100000 + 1)) + "&amp;ver=" + this.Version + "&amp;referrerUrl=" + encodeURIComponent(referrerUrl) + "&amp;fingerPrint=" + fingerPrint + (this.SubID.length &gt; 0 ? "&amp;subId=" + this.SubID : ""), +"&amp;abr=" + g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.IsAdblockRequest, true);
                                }

                                // Append lotame/comscore pixel scripts if required
                                setupTracking();

                                this.Script.Load(function() {
                                    if (typeof _this.Media.Items == "undefined" || _this.Media.Items === undefined || _this.Media.Items === null)
                                        return;

                                    if (_this.IsClientSideFiltersPassed()) {
                                        for (var i = 0; i &lt; _this.Media.Items.length; i++) {
                                            _this.Script.Add(_this.CDNHost + "/Scripts/MediaScripts/" + _this.Media.Items[i].ScriptUri, true);
                                        }

                                        _this.Script.Load(function() {

                                            var mediaType = "";

                                            for (var i = 0; i &lt; _this.Media.Items.length; i++) {

                                                mediaType = _this.Media.Items[i].MediaType;

                                                if (typeof _this.Modules[mediaType] != "undefined") {
                                                    _this.Modules[mediaType](_this.Media.Items[i], _this._Top);
                                                }
                                            }
                                        });
                                    }

                                    g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.Lotame.PlacePixel();
                                    g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.Lotame.PlaceMappingPixel();
                                    g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.Lotame.CallExtractionAPI();
                                    g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PubMatic.PlaceMappingPixel();
                                });
                                if (typeof(InfCustomerCallback) === "function") {
                                    InfCustomerCallback();
                                }
                            } catch (err) {
                                console.log(err);
                                g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.LogError(err);
                            }
                        },

                        IsClientSideFiltersPassed: function() {
                            return true;
                        },

                        FindPublisherSiteFilterLogIndex: function() {
                            var index = -1;

                            for (var i = 0; i &lt; this.Media.DecisionProfile.Log.Messages.length; i++) {
                                if (this.Media.DecisionProfile.Log.Messages[i].Message == "Checking Filters") {
                                    index = i;
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                            return index;
                        },

                        IsPublisherSiteFrequencyCapPassed: function(filter, siteVisitHistory, loggingEnabled) {
                            var numVisits = 0;
                            for (var i in siteVisitHistory) {
                                var visitDate = new Date(siteVisitHistory[i].D);
                                var secondsPassed = (this.ServerDate - visitDate) / 1000;
                                if (secondsPassed &lt; filter.CapLengthInSeconds) {
                                    numVisits++;
                                }
                            }

                            var result = {
                                passed: numVisits &lt; filter.Cap
                            };

                            if (loggingEnabled) {
                                result.message = "User impressions of " + numVisits + " are " + (result.passed ? "under" : "over") + " publisher site frequency cap: " + filter.Cap;
                            }

                            return result;
                        },

                        FetchMediaUrl: function(media, hosted) {
                            var infinityHost = g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.InfinityHost;
                            if (media.Redirect == 1)
                                infinityHost = this.InfinityHost.replace("http://", "https://");

                            var url = this._Top.location;
                            var redirectUrl;

                            if (g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.IsAdblockRequest) {
                                var encodedUrl = g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.b32encode(encodeURIComponent(url));

                                redirectUrl =
                                    "/" + (media.MediaSegmentId ? media.MediaSegmentId : "null") // MediaSegmentId, has to be passed in url, not stored in mongo
                                    + "/" + "null" // (encodedUrl ? encodedUrl : "null") // currentUrl
                                    + "/" + (media.TempMediaId ? media.TempMediaId : "null") // TempMediaId
                                    + "/" + (media.PassBackId ? media.PassBackId : "null") // PassBackId
                                    + "/" + (media.RequestValidationId ? media.RequestValidationId : "null") // Request Validation Id
                                    + "/" + (media.VolumeMetricId ? media.VolumeMetricId : "null") // Request Validation Id
                                    + "/" + (g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.IsAdblockRequest) + "/" + "Redirect.rb";
                            } else {
                                redirectUrl = media.RedirectUrl + "&amp;abr=" + g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.IsAdblockRequest + "&amp;currentUrl=" + encodeURIComponent(url);
                            }

                            if (hosted === true &amp;&amp; media.Settings.Width &lt; 1024) {
                                if (g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.DFPImpressionUrl != undefined &amp;&amp; g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.DFPImpressionUrl != "") {
                                    var bridgeRedirect = "/Bridge/Index?width=" + media.Settings.Width + "&amp;height=" + media.Settings.Height + "&amp;url=" + encodeURIComponent(encodeURIComponent(redirectUrl));
                                    return g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.DFPImpressionUrl + infinityHost + bridgeRedirect;
                                } else {
                                    var bridgeRedirect = "/Bridge/Index?width=" + media.Settings.Width + "&amp;height=" + media.Settings.Height + "&amp;url=" + encodeURIComponent(redirectUrl);
                                    return infinityHost + bridgeRedirect;
                                }
                            }


                            if (media.MediaType === "Link" &amp;&amp; media.Settings["PassParams"] === true &amp;&amp; g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PassParams.length &gt; 0) {
                                var newRedirectUrl = redirectUrl + "&amp;" + g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.PassParams;
                                if (newRedirectUrl.length &lt;= 2048)
                                    redirectUrl = newRedirectUrl;
                                redirectUrl = g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.DFPImpressionUrl + redirectUrl;
                            }

                            var sourceType = g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.MediaSourceTypes;
                            if (media.MediaType === "Link" &amp;&amp; (media.MediaSourceType == sourceType.Video || media.MediaSourceType == sourceType.VideoTag)) {
                                redirectUrl = "/Bridge/Index?width=" + media.Settings.Width + "&amp;height=" + media.Settings.Height + "&amp;url=" + encodeURIComponent(redirectUrl);
                            }

                            // Record impressions
                            g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.Lotame.PlaceImpressionPixel(media);

                            if (g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.EncodeUrl !== undefined &amp;&amp; g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.EncodeUrl) {
                                infinityHost = infinityHost.replace("https://", "").replace("http://", "").replace("//", "");
                                return g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.DFPImpressionUrl + "//" + window.getUri(infinityHost + redirectUrl);
                            }
                            return g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.DFPImpressionUrl + infinityHost + redirectUrl;
                        },

                        IsDontTriggerForSelectorMatch: function(selector, element) {
                            var PARENT_LEVEL = 5;
                            if (selector) {
                                var selectorElements = g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F._Top.document.querySelectorAll(selector);

                                for (var i = 0; i &lt; selectorElements.length; i++) {
                                    var selectedElement = element;
                                    for (var j = 0; j &lt; PARENT_LEVEL; j++) {
                                        if (selectorElements[i] === selectedElement) {
                                            return true;
                                        } else if (selectedElement &amp;&amp; selectedElement.nodeName.toLowerCase() !== "html") {
                                            selectedElement = selectedElement.parentNode;
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            return false;
                        },

                        BindOnDocumentTouch: function(handler) {
                            // trigger on document.click
                            var topWindow = g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F._Top;
                            if (topWindow.document.addEventListener) {

                                        handler(e);
                                    } catch (err) {
                                        g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.LogError(err);
                                    }
                                }, false);
                            } else {
                                try {
                                    topWindow.document.attachEvent("touchstart", handler);
                                } catch (err) {
                                    g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.LogError(err);
                                }
                            }
                        },

                        GetExpiration: function(numSeconds) {
                            var utcMilliSeconds = (new Date()).valueOf() + numSeconds * 1000;
                            var expires = new Date();
                            expires.setTime(utcMilliSeconds);
                            return expires;
                        },

                        IsExpired: function(experationDate) {
                            var current = new Date();
                            var isExpired = current.valueOf() &gt;= Date.parse(experationDate);
                            return isExpired;
                        },

                        IsCapped: function(counterName, expirationName, cap, useSession) {
                            useSession = !!useSession; // defaults to false
                            var capCount = useSession ? this.Storage.GetSessionStorage(counterName) : this.Storage.GetLocalStorage(counterName);
                            var capExpiration = useSession ? this.Storage.GetSessionStorage(expirationName) : this.Storage.GetLocalStorage(expirationName);

                            if (capCount === undefined || capCount === 0 || capExpiration === undefined || this.IsExpired(capExpiration) || isNaN(capCount)) {
                                return false;
                            }
                            return cap !== undefined &amp;&amp; capCount &gt;= cap;
                        },

                        IncrementCap: function(counterName, expirationName, capLength, useSession) {
                            useSession = !!useSession; // defaults to false
                            var capCount = useSession ? this.Storage.GetSessionStorage(counterName) : this.Storage.GetLocalStorage(counterName);
                            var capExpiration = useSession ? this.Storage.GetSessionStorage(expirationName) : this.Storage.GetLocalStorage(expirationName);

                            if (capCount === undefined || capCount === 0 || capExpiration === undefined || this.IsExpired(capExpiration) || isNaN(capCount)) {
                                capCount = 0;
                                capExpiration = this.GetExpiration(capLength);
                            }

                            useSession ? this.Storage.SetSessionStorage(counterName, ++capCount) : this.Storage.SetLocalStorage(counterName, ++capCount);
                            useSession ? this.Storage.SetSessionStorage(expirationName, capExpiration) : this.Storage.SetLocalStorage(expirationName, capExpiration);
                        },

                        IsFastPopCapped: function() {
                            return this.IsCapped("InfNumFastPops", "InfNumFastPopsExpire", this.PopSettings.Cap);
                        },

                        IncrementFastPopCap: function() {
                            this.IncrementCap("InfNumFastPops", "InfNumFastPopsExpire", this.PopSettings.CapLength);
                        },

                        GetWindowHeight: function() {

                            var myHeight = 0;

                            if (typeof(this._Top.window.innerHeight) == 'number') {
                                //Non-IE
                                myHeight = this._Top.window.innerHeight;
                            } else if (this._Top.document.documentElement &amp;&amp; this._Top.document.documentElement.clientHeight) {
                                //IE 6+ in 'standards compliant mode'
                                myHeight = this._Top.document.documentElement.clientHeight;
                            } else if (this._Top.document.body &amp;&amp; this._Top.document.body.clientHeight) {
                                //IE 4 compatible
                                myHeight = this._Top.document.body.clientHeight;
                            }

                            return myHeight;

                        },
                        GetWindowWidth: function() {

                            var myWidth = 0;

                            if (typeof(this._Top.window.innerWidth) == 'number') {
                                //Non-IE
                                myWidth = this._Top.window.innerWidth;
                            } else if (this._Top.document.documentElement &amp;&amp; this._Top.document.documentElement.clientWidth) {
                                //IE 6+ in 'standards compliant mode'
                                myWidth = this._Top.document.documentElement.clientWidth;
                            } else if (this._Top.document.body &amp;&amp; this._Top.document.body.clientWidth) {
                                //IE 4 compatible
                                myWidth = this._Top.document.body.clientWidth;
                            }

                            return myWidth;
                        },
                        GetWindowTop: function() {
                            return (this._Top.window.screenTop !== undefined) ? this._Top.window.screenTop : this._Top.window.screenY;
                        },
                        GetWindowLeft: function() {
                            return (this._Top.window.screenLeft !== undefined) ? this._Top.window.screenLeft : this._Top.window.screenX;
                        },
                        GetParentLink: function(srcElement) {
                            var linkElement = srcElement;
                            if (linkElement.getAttribute("target") == null &amp;&amp; linkElement.getAttribute("rel") == null &amp;&amp; linkElement.nodeName.toLowerCase() != "html") {

                                var parentCount = 0;
                                while (linkElement.parentNode &amp;&amp; parentCount &lt;= 4 &amp;&amp; linkElement.nodeName.toLowerCase() != "html") {

                                    parentCount++;
                                    linkElement = linkElement.parentNode;

                                    if (linkElement.nodeName.toLowerCase() === "a" &amp;&amp; linkElement.href !== "") {
                                        break;
                                    }
                                }
                            }

                            return linkElement;
                        },
                        LoadWebFonts: function(documentObj, fontArray) {
                            if (typeof documentObj === "undefined") {
                                documentObj = document;
                            }
                            if (fontArray instanceof Array &amp;&amp; fontArray.length &gt; 0) {
                                WebFontConfig = {
                                    google: {
                                        families: fontArray
                                    }
                                };
                                var wf = documentObj.createElement('script');
                                wf.src = ('https:' == documentObj.location.protocol ? 'https' : 'http') + '://ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/webfont/1/webfont.js';
                                wf.type = 'text/javascript';
                                wf.async = 'true';
                                var s = documentObj.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
                                s.parentNode.insertBefore(wf, s);
                            }
                        },
                        Querystring: {
                            Init: function() {
                                var e;
                                var a = /\+/g; // Regex for replacing addition symbol with a space
                                var r = /([^&amp;=]+)=?([^&amp;]*)/g;
                                var d = function(s) {
                                    return decodeURIComponent(s.replace(a, " "));
                                };
                                var q = window.location.search.substring(1);
                                /* jshint -W084 */
                                while (e = r.exec(q))
                                    this.Params[d(e[1])] = d(e[2]);
                                /* jshint +W084 */
                            },

                            Params: []
                        },

                        Script: {
                            Items: [],

                            Add: function(url, cache) {

                                if (!this.Exists(url)) {
                                    this.Items.push({
                                        "url": url,
                                        "cache": cache,
                                        "complete": false
                                    });
                                    return true;
                                }
                                return false;
                            },

                            Exists: function(url) {

                                for (var i = 0; i &lt; this.Items.length; i++) {
                                    if (this.Items[i].url == url)
                                        return true;
                                }
                                return false;
                            },

                            Complete: function(items) {

                                for (var i = 0; i &lt; items.length; i++) {
                                    if (!items[i].complete)
                                        return false;
                                }
                                return true;
                            },

                            Create: function(url, cache) {

                                var script = document.createElement("script");
                                script.setAttribute("type", "text/javascript");

                                if (cache) {
                                    script.src = url;
                                } else {
                                    var rand = Math.floor(89999999 * Math.random() + 10000000);
                                    script.src = (url.indexOf("?") &gt; -1) ? url + "&amp;" + rand : url + "?" + rand;
                                }

                                return script;
                            },

                            AppendToDom: function(items, index, callback) {

                                var _this = this;
                                var head = document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0];

                                if (g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.UseAjax !== undefined &amp;&amp; g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.UseAjax) {

                                    g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.AjaxLoad(items[index].url, function(xhr) {
                                        var s = document.createElement("script");
                                        s.type = "text/javascript";
                                        s.innerHTML = xhr.responseText;

                                        var e = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
                                        e.parentNode.insertBefore(s, e);

                                        items[index].complete = true;
                                        if (_this.Complete(items) &amp;&amp; typeof callback == "function") {
                                            callback();
                                        }
                                    });

                                } else {
                                    var thisUrl = items[index].url;
                                    if (g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.EncodeUrl !== undefined &amp;&amp; g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.EncodeUrl) {
                                        thisUrl = "//" + window.getUri(thisUrl);
                                    }
                                    var script = this.Create(thisUrl, items[index].cache);

                                    script.onload = script.onreadystatechange = function(e) {
                                        if (!items[index].complete &amp;&amp; (!this.readyState || this.readyState == "loaded" || this.readyState == "complete")) {

                                            items[index].complete = true;
                                            script.onload = script.onreadystatechange = null;

                                            if (_this.Complete(items) &amp;&amp; typeof callback == "function") {
                                                callback();
                                            }
                                        }
                                    };
                                    head.appendChild(script);
                                }
                            },

                            Load: function(arg1, arg2, arg3) {
                                if (arguments.length === 0 || arguments.length === 1) {
                                    var items = this.Items;
                                    this.Items = [];
                                    for (var i = 0; i &lt; items.length; i++) {
                                        this.AppendToDom(items, i, arg1);
                                    }
                                } else {
                                    this.AppendToDom([{
                                        "url": arg1,
                                        "cache": arg2,
                                        "complete": false
                                    }], 0, arg3);
                                }
                            }
                        },
