                        GetSettingAsInt: function(settings, key, fallback, min, max) {
                            if (fallback === null || fallback === undefined || isNaN(parseInt(fallback))) {
                                fallback = 0;
                            }
                            if (min === null || min === undefined || isNaN(parseInt(min))) {
                                min = false;
                            }
                            if (max === null || max === undefined || isNaN(parseInt(max))) {
                                max = false;
                            }
                            var value = parseInt(fallback);
                            if (settings.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
                                value = parseInt(settings[key], 10);
                                if (isNaN(value)) {
                                    value = parseInt(fallback);
                                }
                            }
                            if (min !== false &amp;&amp; value &lt; min) {
                                value = min;
                            } else if (max !== false &amp;&amp; value &gt; max) {
                                value = max;
                            }
                            return value;
                        },
                        GetSettingAsBool: function(Settings, key, fallback) {
                            var value = false;
                            if (fallback === true || fallback === "true" || fallback === 1 || fallback === "1") {
                                value = true;
                            }
                            if (Settings.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
                                value = Settings[key];
                                if (value === true || value === "true" || value === 1 || value === "1") {
                                    value = true;
                                } else {
                                    value = false;
                                }
                            }
                            return value;
                        },
                        GetSettingAsStr: function(Settings, key, fallback, decodeBool) {
                            if (fallback === null || fallback === undefined) {
                                fallback = "";
                            }
                            if (decodeBool !== true) {
                                decodeBool = false;
                            }
                            var value = fallback;
                            if (Settings.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
                                value = Settings[key];
                                if (value === null || value === undefined) {
                                    value = fallback;
                                }
                            }
                            if (decodeBool) {
                                value = decodeURIComponent(value);
                            }
                            return value;
                        },
                        Storage: {
                            GetLocalStorage: function(name) {
                                var value;
                                if (this.SupportsLocalStorage()) {
                                    value = localStorage[name];
                                } else {
                                    value = this.GetCookie(name);
                                }

                                // Remove the ISSH prefix before returning the value.
                                if (value) {
                                    var prefix = value.split("__")[0];
                                    if (prefix == this.GetCookie("ISSH") || prefix == "undefined") {
                                        value = value.split("__")[1];
                                    }
                                }

                                return value;
                            },
                            SetLocalStorage: function(name, value) {
                                // We're not entirely sure why we're prefixing the value with
                                // the ISSH cookie value.
                                var prefixedValue = this.GetCookie("ISSH") + "__" + value;
                                if (this.SupportsLocalStorage()) {
                                    try {
                                        localStorage[name] = prefixedValue;
                                    } catch (err) {
                                        this.FailedLocalStorage = true;
                                        return;
                                    }
                                } else {
                                    this.SetCookie(name, prefixedValue);
                                }
                            },
                            SupportsLocalStorage: function() {
                                try {
                                    sessionStorage.setItem('storageSupport', 1);
                                    sessionStorage.removeItem('storageSupport');
                                    return 'localStorage' in window &amp;&amp; window['localStorage'] !== null;
                                } catch (err) {
                                    if (err.code === DOMException.QUOTA_EXCEEDED_ERR &amp;&amp; sessionStorage.length === 0) {
                                        window.console = window.console || {
                                            log: function(d) {}
                                        };
                                        console.log("Safari private mode detected");
                                    }
                                    return false;
                                }
                            },
                            GetSessionStorage: function(name) {
                                var value;
                                if (this.SupportsSessionStorage()) {
                                    value = sessionStorage[name];
                                } else {
                                    value = this.GetCookie(name);
                                }

                                // Remove the ISSH prefix before returning the value.
                                if (value) {
                                    var prefix = value.split("__")[0];
                                    if (prefix == this.GetCookie("ISSH") || prefix == "undefined") {
                                        value = value.split("__")[1];
                                    }
                                }

                                return value;
                            },
                            SetSessionStorage: function(name, value) {
                                // We're not entirely sure why we're prefixing the value with
                                // the ISSH cookie value.
                                var prefixedValue = this.GetCookie("ISSH") + "__" + value;
                                if (this.SupportsSessionStorage()) {
                                    try {
                                        sessionStorage[name] = prefixedValue;
                                    } catch (err) {
                                        this.FailedSessionStorage = true;
                                        // g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.LogError(err);
                                    }
                                } else {
                                    this.SetCookie(name, prefixedValue);
                                }
                            },
                            GetSiteVisitHistory: function(siteId) {
                                try {
                                    var rawCookie = this.GetCookie("ISPH").substring(1);

                                    rawCookie = rawCookie.replace(/~1/g, "[{\"")
                                        .replace(/~E/g, "SId\":")
                                        .replace(/~4/g, "\"D\"")
                                        .replace(/~3/g, "\"SId\"")
                                        .replace(/~C/g, "\"2014-")
                                        .replace(/~D/g, "\"2015-")
                                        .replace(/~2/g, "\"}]");

                                    eval("var siteVisitHistory = " + rawCookie);
                                    return siteVisitHistory[siteId];
                                } catch (err) {
                                    g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.LogError(err);
                                    return null;
                                }
                            },

                            SupportsSessionStorage: function() {
                                try {
                                    sessionStorage.setItem('storageSupport', 1);
                                    sessionStorage.removeItem('storageSupport');
                                    return 'sessionStorage' in window &amp;&amp; window['sessionStorage'] !== null;
                                } catch (err) {
                                    if (err.code === DOMException.QUOTA_EXCEEDED_ERR &amp;&amp; sessionStorage.length === 0) {
                                        window.console = window.console || {
                                            log: function(d) {}
                                        };
                                        console.log("Safari private mode detected");
                                    }
                                    // g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.LogError(err);
                                    return false;
                                }
                            },
                            SetCookie: function(c_name, value, seconds) {
                                var exdate = new Date();
                                exdate.setSeconds(exdate.getSeconds() + seconds);
                                var c_value = escape(value) + ((seconds == null) ? "" : "; expires=" + exdate.toUTCString());
                                document.cookie = c_name + "=" + c_value;
                            },
                            GetCookie: function(c_name) {
                                var i, x, y, ARRcookies = document.cookie.split(";");
                                for (i = 0; i &lt; ARRcookies.length; i++) {
                                    x = ARRcookies[i].substr(0, ARRcookies[i].indexOf("="));
                                    y = ARRcookies[i].substr(ARRcookies[i].indexOf("=") + 1);
                                    x = x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, "");
                                    if (x == c_name) {
                                        return unescape(y);
                                    }
                                }
                            },
                            FailedLocalStorage: false,
                            FailedSessionStorage: false
                        },

                        StopEvent: function(e) {
                            if (e.preventDefault) {
                                e.preventDefault();
                            }
                            if (e.stopImmediatePropagation) {
                                e.stopImmediatePropagation();
                            }
                            if (e.stopPropagation) {
                                e.stopPropagation();
                            }
                        },

                        /* http://www.abeautifulsite.net/blog/2011/11/detecting-mobile-devices-with-javascript/ */
                        IsMobile: {
                            Android: function(targetWindow) {
                                return targetWindow.navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i);
                            },
                            BlackBerry: function(targetWindow) {
                                return targetWindow.navigator.userAgent.match(/BlackBerry/i);
                            },
                            iOS: function(targetWindow) {
                                return targetWindow.navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone|iPad|iPod/i);
                            },
                            Opera: function(targetWindow) {
                                return targetWindow.navigator.userAgent.match(/Opera Mini/i);
                            },
                            Windows: function(targetWindow) {
                                return targetWindow.navigator.userAgent.match(/IEMobile/i);
                            },
                            any: function(targetWindow) {
                                return targetWindow.navigator.userAgent.match(/Android|BlackBerry|iPhone|iPad|iPod|Opera Mini|IEMobile/i);
                            }
                        },

                        Browser: new function() {
                            var _browser = this;
                            // Gets browser instance parsed using UAParser
                            this.current = new UAParser().getBrowser();
                            // Browsers
                            this.isSafari = function() {
                                return _browser.current.name === 'Safari';
                            };
                            this.isChrome = function() {
                                return _browser.current.name === 'Chrome';
                            };
                            this.isOpera = function() {
                                return _browser.current.name === 'Opera';
                            };
                            this.isFirefox = function() {
                                return _browser.current.name === 'Firefox';
                            };
                            this.isIE = function() {
                                return _browser.current.name === 'IE';
                            };

                            return _browser;
                        },

                        b32encode: function(s) {
                            /* encodes a string s to base32 and returns the encoded string */
                            var alphabet = "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ234567";

                            var parts = [];
                            var quanta = Math.floor((s.length / 5));
                            var leftover = s.length % 5;

                            if (leftover != 0) {
                                for (var i = 0; i &lt; (5 - leftover); i++) {
                                    s += '\x00';
                                }
                                quanta += 1;
                            }

                            for (i = 0; i &lt; quanta; i++) {
                                parts.push(alphabet.charAt(s.charCodeAt(i * 5) &gt;&gt; 3));
                                parts.push(alphabet.charAt(((s.charCodeAt(i * 5) &amp; 0x07) &lt;&lt; 2) | (s.charCodeAt(i * 5 + 1) &gt;&gt; 6)));
                                parts.push(alphabet.charAt(((s.charCodeAt(i * 5 + 1) &amp; 0x3F) &gt;&gt; 1)));
                                parts.push(alphabet.charAt(((s.charCodeAt(i * 5 + 1) &amp; 0x01) &lt;&lt; 4) | (s.charCodeAt(i * 5 + 2) &gt;&gt; 4)));
                                parts.push(alphabet.charAt(((s.charCodeAt(i * 5 + 2) &amp; 0x0F) &lt;&lt; 1) | (s.charCodeAt(i * 5 + 3) &gt;&gt; 7)));
                                parts.push(alphabet.charAt(((s.charCodeAt(i * 5 + 3) &amp; 0x7F) &gt;&gt; 2)));
                                parts.push(alphabet.charAt(((s.charCodeAt(i * 5 + 3) &amp; 0x03) &lt;&lt; 3) | (s.charCodeAt(i * 5 + 4) &gt;&gt; 5)));
                                parts.push(alphabet.charAt(((s.charCodeAt(i * 5 + 4) &amp; 0x1F))));
                            }

                            var replace = 0;
                            if (leftover == 1) replace = 6;
                            else if (leftover == 2) replace = 4;
                            else if (leftover == 3) replace = 3;
                            else if (leftover == 4) replace = 1;

                            for (i = 0; i &lt; replace; i++) parts.pop();

                            return parts.join("");
                        },
                        AjaxLoad: function(url, callback) {
                            // the callback contains the xhr object from which the response text
                            // can be retrieved using the responseText property
                            var xhr;
                            if (typeof XMLHttpRequest !== "undefined") {
                                xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
                            } else {
                                var versions = [
                                    "MSXML2.XmlHttp.5.0",
                                    "MSXML2.XmlHttp.4.0",
                                    "MSXML2.XmlHttp.3.0",
                                    "MSXML2.XmlHttp.2.0",
                                    "Microsoft.XmlHttp"
                                ];
                                for (var i = 0, len = versions.length; i &lt; len; i++) {
                                    try {
                                        xhr = new ActiveXObject(versions[i]);
                                        break;
                                    } catch (e) {}
                                }
                            }
                            var ensureReadiness = function() {
                                if (xhr.readyState &lt; 4) {
                                    return;
                                }
                                if (xhr.status !== 200) {
                                    return;
                                }
                                if (xhr.readyState === 4) {
                                    callback(xhr);
                                }
                            };
                            xhr.onreadystatechange = ensureReadiness;
                            xhr.open("GET", url, true);
                            xhr.send();
                        },
                        AjaxPost: function(url, payload, optionalHeaders, callback) {
                            // the callback contains the xhr object from which the response text
                            // can be retrieved using the responseText property
                            var xhr;
                            if (typeof XMLHttpRequest !== "undefined") {
                                xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
                            } else {
                                var versions = [
                                    "MSXML2.XmlHttp.5.0",
                                    "MSXML2.XmlHttp.4.0",
                                    "MSXML2.XmlHttp.3.0",
                                    "MSXML2.XmlHttp.2.0",
                                    "Microsoft.XmlHttp"
                                ];
                                for (var i = 0, len = versions.length; i &lt; len; i++) {
                                    try {
                                        xhr = new ActiveXObject(versions[i]);
                                        break;
                                    } catch (e) {}
                                }
                            }
                            var ensureReadiness = function() {
                                if (xhr.readyState &lt; 4) {
                                    return;
                                }
                                if (xhr.status !== 202) {
                                    return;
                                }
                                if (xhr.readyState === 4) {
                                    typeof callback === "function" &amp;&amp; callback(xhr);
                                }
                            };
                            xhr.onreadystatechange = ensureReadiness;
                            xhr.open("POST", url, true);
                            if (optionalHeaders &amp;&amp; optionalHeaders.length &gt; 0) {
                                for (var i = 0; i &lt; optionalHeaders.length; i++) {
                                    xhr.setRequestHeader(optionalHeaders[i].header, optionalHeaders[i].value);
                                }
                            }
                            xhr.send(payload);
                        },

                        ExternalChromePop: function() {

                            window.console = window.console || {
                                log: function(d) {}
                            };
                            return function() {

                                try {

                                    var g = g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F;

                                    g.FlashElem.style.width = "0px";
                                    g.FlashElem.style.height = "0px";
                                    g.FlashElem.style.visibility = "hidden";

                                    var triggerClick = function(link) {
                                        if (link.tagName.toLowerCase() !== "input" &amp;&amp; link.tagName.toLowerCase() !== "textarea" &amp;&amp; link.tagName.toLowerCase() !== "option" || link.focus()) {
                                            link.click();
                                        }
                                    };

                                    var reInit = function() {
                                        g.FlashElem.style.width = "1px";
                                        g.FlashElem.style.height = "1px";
                                        g.FlashElem.style.visibility = "visible";
                                        g.FlashElem.style.position = "fixed";
                                        g.FlashElem.style.left = "0";
                                        g.FlashElem.style.top = "0";
                                    }

                                    var link = g._Top.document.elementFromPoint(g.MousePosX, g.MousePosY);
                                    g.OriginalLink = link;

                                    if (link.nodeName.toLowerCase() !== "a") {
                                        link = g.GetParentLink(link);
                                    }

                                    if (g.IsFastPop) {

                                        if (g.PopRunning) {
                                            triggerClick(link);
                                            return;
                                        }

                                        if (g.PopLoaded || g.IsFastPopCapped()) {
                                            triggerClick(link);
                                            return;
                                        }

                                        if (g.IsDontTriggerForSelectorMatch(g.PopSettings.PopUnderDontTriggerSelector, g.OriginalLink)) {
                                            triggerClick(link);
                                            reInit();
                                            return;
                                        }

                                        if (g.PopSettings.RespectTargetBlank &amp;&amp; (link.getAttribute("target") === "_blank" || link.getAttribute("rel") === "nofollow")) {
                                            triggerClick(link);
                                            reInit();
                                            return;
                                        }

                                        g.PopRunning = true;

                                    } else {
                                        if (g.IsCapped("InfNumPops" + g.PopMedia.ZoneId, "InfNumPopsExpire" + g.PopMedia.ZoneId, g.PopMedia.Settings.cap)) {
                                            triggerClick(link);
                                            return;
                                        }
                                        if (g.PopMedia.Settings.RespectTargetBlank &amp;&amp; (link.getAttribute("target") === "_blank" || link.getAttribute("rel") === "nofollow")) {
                                            triggerClick(link);
                                            reInit();
                                            return;
                                        }
                                        if (g.IsDontTriggerForSelectorMatch(g.PopMedia.Settings.PopUnderDontTriggerSelector, g.OriginalLink)) {
                                            triggerClick(link);
                                            reInit();
                                            return;
                                        }
                                        g.IncrementCap("InfNumPops" + g.PopMedia.ZoneId, "InfNumPopsExpire" + g.PopMedia.ZoneId, g.PopMedia.Settings.capLength);
                                    }

                                    window.open(g.PopMediaUrl, Math.floor((Math.random() * 1e3) + 1), g.PopMediaOptions);
                                    setTimeout(function() {
                                        triggerClick(link);
                                        g.PopLoaded = true;
                                        g.PopRunning = false;
                                        if (g.IsFastPop) {
                                            g.IncrementFastPopCap();
                                        }
                                    }, 75);
                                } catch (err) {
                                    g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F.LogError(err);
                                }
                            }();
                        },
                        LogError: function(ex) {
                            var g36 = g367CB268B1094004A3689751E7AC568F;

                            var getViewPort = function() {
                                var e = g36._Top.document.documentElement,
                                    g = g36._Top.document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0],
                                    x = g36._Top.window.innerWidth || e.clientWidth || g.clientWidth,
                                    y = g36._Top.window.innerHeight || e.clientHeight || g.clientHeight;
                                return {
                                    width: x,
                                    height: y
                                };
                            };

                            var stackTrace = g36.ComputeStackTrace(ex);

                            if (stackTrace.mode !== "failed") {
                                var stack = [];
                                if (stackTrace.stack &amp;&amp; stackTrace.stack.length) {
                                    for (var i = 0; i &lt; stackTrace.stack.length; i++) {
                                        var frame = stackTrace.stack[i];
                                        stack.push({
                                            'LineNumber': frame.line,
                                            'ColumnNumber': frame.column,
                                            'ClassName': 'line ' + frame.line + ', column ' + frame.column,
                                            'FileName': frame.url,
                                            'MethodName': frame.func || '[anonymous]'
                                        });
                                    }
                                }

                                var url = g36.RaygunUrl;

                                var qs = {};
                                var queryString = g36.ParseUrl('?');
                                if (queryString.length &gt; 0) {
                                    var segments = queryString.split('&amp;');
                                    for (var i = 0; i &lt; segments.length; i++) {
                                        var segment = segments[i];
                                        var parts = segment.split('=');
                                        if (parts &amp;&amp; parts.length === 2) {
                                            var key = decodeURIComponent(parts[0]);
                                            var value = parts[1];
                                            qs[key] = value;
                                        }
                                    }
                                }

                                var payload = {
                                    'occurredOn': new Date(),
                                    'details': {
                                        'error': {
                                            'className': stackTrace.name,
                                            'message': stackTrace.message,
                                            'stackTrace': stack
                                        },
                                        'environment': {
                                            'UtcOffset': new Date().getTimezoneOffset() / -60.0,
                                            'User-Language': g36._Top.navigator.userLanguage,
                                            'Document-Mode': g36._Top.document.documentMode,
                                            'Browser-Width': getViewPort().width,
                                            'Browser-Height': getViewPort().height,
                                            'Screen-Width': g36._Top.screen.width,
                                            'Screen-Height': g36._Top.screen.height,
                                            'Color-Depth': g36._Top.screen.colorDepth,
                                            'Browser': g36._Top.navigator.appCodeName,
                                            'Browser-Name': g36._Top.navigator.appName,
                                            'Browser-Version': g36._Top.navigator.appVersion,
                                            'Platform': g36._Top.navigator.platform
                                        },
                                        'request': {
                                            'url': [g36._Top.location.protocol, '//', g36._Top.location.host, g36._Top.location.pathname, g36._Top.location.hash].join(''),
                                            'querystring': qs,
                                            'ipAddress': g36.ClientIP,
                                            'headers': {
                                                'user-agent': g36._Top.navigator.userAgent,
                                                'referer': g36._Top.document.referrer,
                                                'host': g36._Top.document.domain
                                            }
                                        },
                                        'user': {
                                            'identifier': g36.SiteId,
                                            'fullName': g36.SiteName
                                        }
                                    }
                                };
                                g36.AjaxPost(url, JSON.stringify(payload), null, function(xhr) {
                                    console.log("INF: error logged successfully", xhr.responseText);
                                });
                            } else {
                                console.log("INF: cannot parse error stack");
                            }
                        },
                        /*
                        TraceKit - Cross brower stack traces - github.com/occ/TraceKit
                        MIT license
                        */
                        ComputeStackTrace: (function computeStackTraceWrapper() {
                            function n(n, e) {
                                return Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(n, e)
                            }

                            function e(n) {
                                return "undefined" == typeof n
                            }

                            function t(n) {
                                return ""
                            }

                            function r(e) {
                                if (!n(w, e)) {
                                    var r = "";
                                    e = e || "", e.indexOf &amp;&amp; -1 !== e.indexOf(document.domain) &amp;&amp; (r = t(e)), w[e] = r ? r.split("\n") : []
                                }
                                return w[e]
                            }

                            function l(n, t) {
                                var l, i = /function ([^(]*)\(([^)]*)\)/,
                                    u = /['"]?([0-9A-Za-z$_]+)['"]?\s*[:=]\s*(function|eval|new Function)/,
                                    c = "",
                                    s = 10,
                                    a = r(n);
                                if (!a.length) return k;
                                for (var o = 0; s &gt; o; ++o)
                                    if (c = a[t - o] + c, !e(c)) {
                                        if (l = u.exec(c)) return l[1];
                                        if (l = i.exec(c)) return l[1]
                                    }
                                return k
                            }

                            function i(n, t) {
                                var l = r(n);
                                if (!l.length) return null;
                                var i = [],
                                    u = Math.floor(5.5),
                                    c = u + 1,
                                    s = Math.max(0, t - u - 1),
                                    a = Math.min(l.length, t + c - 1);
                                t -= 1;
                                for (var o = s; a &gt; o; ++o) e(l[o]) || i.push(l[o]);
                                return i.length &gt; 0 ? i : null
                            }

                            function u(n) {
                                return n.replace(/[\-\[\]{}()*+?.,\\\^$|#]/g, "\\$&amp;")
                            }

                            function c(n) {
                                return u(n).replace("&lt;", "(?:&lt;|&lt;)").replace("&gt;", "(?:&gt;|&gt;)").replace("&amp;", "(?:&amp;|&amp;)").replace('"', '(?:"|&quot;)').replace(/\s+/g, "\\s+")
                            }

                            function s(n, e) {
                                for (var t, l, i = 0, u = e.length; u &gt; i; ++i)
                                    if ((t = r(e[i])).length &amp;&amp; (t = t.join("\n"), l = n.exec(t))) return {
                                        url: e[i],
                                        line: t.substring(0, l.index).split("\n").length,
                                        column: l.index - t.lastIndexOf("\n", l.index) - 1
                                    };
                                return null
                            }

                            function a(n, e, t) {
                                var l, i = r(e),
                                    c = new RegExp("\\b" + u(n) + "\\b");
                                return t -= 1, i &amp;&amp; i.length &gt; t &amp;&amp; (l = c.exec(i[t])) ? l.index : null
                            }

                            function o(n) {
                                for (var e, t, r, l, i = [window.location.href], a = document.getElementsByTagName("script"), o = "" + n, f = /^function(?:\s+([\w$]+))?\s*\(([\w\s,]*)\)\s*\{\s*(\S[\s\S]*\S)\s*\}\s*$/, p = /^function on([\w$]+)\s*\(event\)\s*\{\s*(\S[\s\S]*\S)\s*\}\s*$/, g = 0; g &lt; a.length; ++g) {
                                    var m = a[g];
                                    m.src &amp;&amp; i.push(m.src)
                                }
                                if (r = f.exec(o)) {
                                    var h = r[1] ? "\\s+" + r[1] : "",
                                        x = r[2].split(",").join("\\s*,\\s*");
                                    e = u(r[3]).replace(/;$/, ";?"), t = new RegExp("function" + h + "\\s*\\(\\s*" + x + "\\s*\\)\\s*{\\s*" + e + "\\s*}")
                                } else t = new RegExp(u(o).replace(/\s+/g, "\\s+"));
                                if (l = s(t, i)) return l;
                                if (r = p.exec(o)) {
                                    var d = r[1];
                                    if (e = c(r[2]), t = new RegExp("on" + d + "=[\\'\"]\\s*" + e + "\\s*[\\'\"]", "i"), l = s(t, i[0])) return l;
                                    if (t = new RegExp(e), l = s(t, i)) return l
                                }
                                return null
                            }

                            function f(n) {
                                if (!n.stack) return null;
                                for (var e, t, r = /^\s*at (?:((?:\[object object\])?\S+(?: \[as \S+\])?) )?\(?((?:file|http|https|chrome-extension):.*?):(\d+)(?::(\d+))?\)?\s*$/i, u = /^\s*(\S*)(?:\((.*?)\))?@?((?:file|http|https):.*?):(\d+)(?::(\d+))?\s*$/i, c = /^\s*at (?:((?:\[object object\])?.+) )?\(?((?:ms-appx|http|https):.*?):(\d+)(?::(\d+))?\)?\s*$/i, s = n.stack.split("\n"), o = [], f = /^(.*) is undefined$/.exec(n.message), p = 0, g = s.length; g &gt; p; ++p) {
                                    if (e = u.exec(s[p])) t = {
                                        url: e[3],
                                        func: e[1] || k,
                                        args: e[2] ? e[2].split(",") : "",
                                        line: +e[4],
                                        column: e[5] ? +e[5] : null
                                    };
                                    else if (e = r.exec(s[p])) t = {
                                        url: e[2],
                                        func: e[1] || k,
                                        line: +e[3],
                                        column: e[4] ? +e[4] : null
                                    };
                                    else {
                                        if (!(e = c.exec(s[p]))) continue;
                                        t = {
                                            url: e[2],
                                            func: e[1] || k,
                                            line: +e[3],
                                            column: e[4] ? +e[4] : null
                                        }
                                    }!t.func &amp;&amp; t.line &amp;&amp; (t.func = l(t.url, t.line)), t.line &amp;&amp; (t.context = i(t.url, t.line)), o.push(t)
                                }
                                return o[0] &amp;&amp; o[0].line &amp;&amp; !o[0].column &amp;&amp; f &amp;&amp; (o[0].column = a(f[1], o[0].url, o[0].line)), o.length ? {
                                    mode: "stack",
                                    name: n.name,
                                    message: n.message,
                                    url: document.location.href,
                                    stack: o,
                                    useragent: navigator.userAgent
                                } : null
                            }

                            function p(n) {
                                for (var e, t = n.stacktrace, r = / line (\d+), column (\d+) in (?:&lt;anonymous function: ([^&gt;]+)&gt;|([^\)]+))\((.*)\) in (.*):\s*$/i, u = t.split("\n"), c = [], s = 0, a = u.length; a &gt; s; s += 2)
                                    if (e = r.exec(u[s])) {
                                        var o = {
                                            line: +e[1],
